# --- Volkswagen ---
pm_volkswagen_autostadt = {
	texture = "gfx/interface/icons/production_method_icons/cat_car_gold_p0.dds"
	state_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			state_infrastructure_mult = 0.1
			goods_output_tourism_mult = 0.1
			state_migration_pull_mult = 0.15
		}
	}
	building_modifiers = {
		workforce_scaled = {
			# Input goods
			goods_input_automobiles_add = 10                     # Price:  100, Total cost:  1000.0 (100.00%)
			# Output goods
			goods_output_merchant_marine_add = 100               # Price:   50, Total cost:  5000.0 (100.00%)
			# Total input cost: 1000.0
			# Total output cost: 5000.0
			# Profit: 4000.0
			# Profit margin: 400.00%
			# Zero profit price multiplier: 0.20
			# Employment: 2000
			# Wage breakeven: 2.00
		}
		level_scaled = {
			building_employment_shopkeepers_add = 800
			building_employment_clerks_add = 800
			building_employment_engineers_add = 200
			building_employment_machinists_add = 200
		}
	}
}
